from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
import triton
import triton.language as tl

OP_TYPE = "kimi_linear_w4a16_decode"
HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000"]
EPS = 1.0e-6
GROUP_SIZE = 128


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class Config:
    hidden: int = 2304
    kda_heads: int = 32
    kda_head_dim: int = 128
    short_conv: int = 4
    mla_heads: int = 32
    kv_lora: int = 512
    qk_nope: int = 128
    qk_rope: int = 64
    v_head: int = 128
    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
    n_experts: int = 64
    n_active: int = 8
    n_shared: int = 1
    moe_inter: int = 1024
    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
    group: int = 128
    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)


def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))


@triton.jit
def _int4_gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                      BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for g in range(0, NG):
        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
        packed = tl.load(wq + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                         mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
        s = tl.load(scales + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zeros + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc += s * (qx - z * xs)

    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _rmsnorm_kernel(x, w, y, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    mask = offs < N
    xv = tl.load(x + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    wv = tl.load(w + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    ss = tl.sum(xv * xv, axis=0) / N
    inv = tl.rsqrt(ss + 1.0e-6)
    tl.store(y + offs, xv * inv * wv, mask=mask)


@triton.jit
def _short_conv_kernel(val, prev, weight, out, new_prev, C: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    offs = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    mask = offs < C
    p0 = tl.load(prev + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p1 = tl.load(prev + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p2 = tl.load(prev + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    x = tl.load(val + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w0 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w1 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w2 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w3 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    y = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + x * w3
    y = y * tl.sigmoid(y)
    tl.store(out + offs, y, mask=mask)
    tl.store(new_prev + offs, p1, mask=mask)
    tl.store(new_prev + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
    tl.store(new_prev + 2 * C + offs, x, mask=mask)


@triton.jit
def _kda_state_kernel(q, k, v, g, beta, S, out,
                      H: tl.constexpr, D: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_DV: tl.constexpr):
    h = tl.program_id(0)
    block_v = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_v = block_v * BLOCK_DV + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_DV)
    mask_v = offs_v < D
    base_h = h * D * D
    base_vec = h * D
    pred = tl.zeros((BLOCK_DV,), tl.float32)

    for dk in range(0, D):
        gg = tl.load(g + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
        kk = tl.load(k + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
        s_old = tl.load(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        pred += (s_old * tl.exp(gg)) * kk

    vv = tl.load(v + base_vec + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    bb = tl.load(beta + h).to(tl.float32)
    oacc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_DV,), tl.float32)

    for dk in range(0, D):
        gg = tl.load(g + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
        kk = tl.load(k + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
        qq = tl.load(q + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
        s_old = tl.load(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        s_new = s_old * tl.exp(gg) + bb * kk * (vv - pred)
        tl.store(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, s_new, mask=mask_v)
        oacc += s_new * qq

    tl.store(out + base_vec + offs_v, oacc, mask=mask_v)


@triton.jit
def _kda_qkvg_kernel(x,
                     wq0, s0, z0, wq1, s1, z1, wq2, s2, z2, wq3, s3, z3, y,
                     K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc2 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc3 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for g in range(0, NG):
        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
        w_offs = (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]

        p0 = tl.load(wq0 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo0 = (p0 & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi0 = ((p0 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx0 = tl.sum(lo0 * xe[:, None] + hi0 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ss0 = tl.load(s0 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zz0 = tl.load(z0 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc0 += ss0 * (qx0 - zz0 * xs)

        p1 = tl.load(wq1 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo1 = (p1 & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi1 = ((p1 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx1 = tl.sum(lo1 * xe[:, None] + hi1 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ss1 = tl.load(s1 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zz1 = tl.load(z1 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc1 += ss1 * (qx1 - zz1 * xs)

        p2 = tl.load(wq2 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo2 = (p2 & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi2 = ((p2 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx2 = tl.sum(lo2 * xe[:, None] + hi2 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ss2 = tl.load(s2 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zz2 = tl.load(z2 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc2 += ss2 * (qx2 - zz2 * xs)

        p3 = tl.load(wq3 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo3 = (p3 & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi3 = ((p3 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx3 = tl.sum(lo3 * xe[:, None] + hi3 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ss3 = tl.load(s3 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zz3 = tl.load(z3 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc3 += ss3 * (qx3 - zz3 * xs)

    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc0, mask=mask_n)
    tl.store(y + N + offs_n, acc1, mask=mask_n)
    tl.store(y + 2 * N + offs_n, acc2, mask=mask_n)
    tl.store(y + 3 * N + offs_n, acc3, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _experts_dual_gemv_kernel(x, idx, wq_a, scales_a, zeros_a, wq_b, scales_b, zeros_b, y_a, y_b,
                              K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                              BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc_a = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc_b = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
    q_base = e * NG * N

    for g in range(0, NG):
        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
        w_offs = w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]

        pa = tl.load(wq_a + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        loa = (pa & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hia = ((pa >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qxa = tl.sum(loa * xe[:, None] + hia * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        sa = tl.load(scales_a + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        za = tl.load(zeros_a + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc_a += sa * (qxa - za * xs)

        pb = tl.load(wq_b + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lob = (pb & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hib = ((pb >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qxb = tl.sum(lob * xe[:, None] + hib * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        sb = tl.load(scales_b + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zb = tl.load(zeros_b + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc_b += sb * (qxb - zb * xs)

    tl.store(y_a + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_a, mask=mask_n)
    tl.store(y_b + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_b, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _experts_down_weighted_kernel(h, coeff, idx, wq, scales, zeros, y,
                                  K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                                  ESEL: tl.constexpr, ADD: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for ep in range(0, ESEL):
        e = tl.load(idx + ep)
        c = tl.load(coeff + ep).to(tl.float32)
        w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
        q_base = e * NG * N
        acc_e = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
        for g in range(0, NG):
            k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
            xe = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
            xo = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
            packed = tl.load(wq + w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                             mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
            lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
            hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
            qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
            xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
            s = tl.load(scales + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            z = tl.load(zeros + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            acc_e += s * (qx - z * xs)
        acc += c * acc_e

    if ADD:
        acc += tl.load(y + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _moe_dual_gemv_kernel(x, idx,
                          wq_a, scales_a, zeros_a, wq_b, scales_b, zeros_b,
                          swq_a, sscales_a, szeros_a, swq_b, sscales_b, szeros_b,
                          y_a, y_b,
                          K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                          ACTIVE: tl.constexpr, SHARED: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    is_routed = pid_e < ACTIVE
    e_r = tl.load(idx + pid_e, mask=is_routed, other=0)
    e_s = pid_e - ACTIVE
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc_a = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc_b = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    w_base_r = e_r * (K // 2) * N
    q_base_r = e_r * NG * N
    w_base_s = e_s * (K // 2) * N
    q_base_s = e_s * NG * N

    for g in range(0, NG):
        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
        w_offs_r = w_base_r + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
        w_offs_s = w_base_s + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
        ptra = tl.where(is_routed, wq_a + w_offs_r, swq_a + w_offs_s)
        ptrb = tl.where(is_routed, wq_b + w_offs_r, swq_b + w_offs_s)

        pa = tl.load(ptra, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        loa = (pa & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hia = ((pa >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qxa = tl.sum(loa * xe[:, None] + hia * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ptra_s = tl.where(is_routed, scales_a + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
                          sscales_a + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
        ptra_z = tl.where(is_routed, zeros_a + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
                          szeros_a + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
        sa = tl.load(ptra_s, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        za = tl.load(ptra_z, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc_a += sa * (qxa - za * xs)

        pb = tl.load(ptrb, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lob = (pb & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hib = ((pb >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qxb = tl.sum(lob * xe[:, None] + hib * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        ptrb_s = tl.where(is_routed, scales_b + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
                          sscales_b + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
        ptrb_z = tl.where(is_routed, zeros_b + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
                          szeros_b + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
        sb = tl.load(ptrb_s, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        zb = tl.load(ptrb_z, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc_b += sb * (qxb - zb * xs)

    tl.store(y_a + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_a, mask=mask_n)
    tl.store(y_b + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_b, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _moe_down_kernel(h, coeff, idx,
                     wq, scales, zeros, swq, sscales, szeros, y,
                     K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                     ACTIVE: tl.constexpr, SHARED: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for ep in range(0, ACTIVE + SHARED):
        if ep < ACTIVE:
            e = tl.load(idx + ep)
            c = tl.load(coeff + ep).to(tl.float32)
            base_w = wq
            base_s = scales
            base_z = zeros
        else:
            e = tl.full((), ep - ACTIVE, tl.int64)
            c = 1.0
            base_w = swq
            base_s = sscales
            base_z = szeros
        w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
        q_base = e * NG * N
        acc_e = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
        for g in range(0, NG):
            k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
            xe = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
            xo = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
            packed = tl.load(base_w + w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                             mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
            lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
            hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
            qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
            xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
            s = tl.load(base_s + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            z = tl.load(base_z + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            acc_e += s * (qx - z * xs)
        acc += c * acc_e

    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)


@triton.jit
def _mla_q_abs_kernel(q, wq, scales, zeros, out,
                      H: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_k = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_k = pid_k * BLOCK_K + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
    offs_j = tl.arange(0, 128)
    mask_k = offs_k < K
    out_cols = pid_h * 256 + offs_j
    qv = tl.load(q + pid_h * 128 + offs_j).to(tl.float32)
    group = offs_k // 128
    packed_row = offs_k // 2
    packed = tl.load(wq + packed_row[:, None] * N + out_cols[None, :], mask=mask_k[:, None], other=0)
    nib = tl.where((offs_k[:, None] & 1) == 0, packed & 15, (packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
    s = tl.load(scales + group[:, None] * N + out_cols[None, :], mask=mask_k[:, None], other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    z = tl.load(zeros + group[:, None] * N + out_cols[None, :], mask=mask_k[:, None], other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    vals = (nib - z) * s
    acc = tl.sum(vals * qv[None, :], axis=1)
    tl.store(out + pid_h * K + offs_k, acc, mask=mask_k)


@triton.jit
def _mla_v_out_kernel(ctx, wq, scales, zeros, out,
                      H: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_n0 = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_n = pid_h * 256 + 128 + offs_n0
    mask_n = offs_n0 < 128
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for g in range(0, 4):
        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
        xe = tl.load(ctx + pid_h * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
        xo = tl.load(ctx + pid_h * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
        packed = tl.load(wq + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                         mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
        lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
        s = tl.load(scales + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zeros + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc += s * (qx - z * xs)

    tl.store(out + pid_h * 128 + offs_n0, acc, mask=mask_n)


def _ceil_div(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    return triton.cdiv(a, b)


def _fused_rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    y = torch.empty_like(x)
    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, y, x.numel(), BLOCK=4096, num_warps=8)
    return y


def _fused_short_conv(val: torch.Tensor, prev: torch.Tensor, weight: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
    out = torch.empty_like(val)
    new_prev = torch.empty_like(prev)
    _short_conv_kernel[(_ceil_div(val.numel(), 256),)](
        val, prev, weight, out, new_prev, val.numel(), BLOCK=256, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out, new_prev


def _fused_kda_state(q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, g: torch.Tensor,
                     beta: torch.Tensor, state_s: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    out = torch.empty((32, 128), device=q.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _kda_state_kernel[(32, 4)](
        q, k, v, g, beta, state_s, out,
        32, 128, BLOCK_DV=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out


def _fused_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, wq: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor,
                in_f: int, out_f: int) -> torch.Tensor:
    y = torch.empty((out_f,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _int4_gemv_kernel[(_ceil_div(out_f, 32),)](
        x, wq, scales, zeros, y, in_f, out_f, in_f // GROUP_SIZE,
        BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return y


def _kda_qkvg(x: torch.Tensor, q, k, v, g) -> torch.Tensor:
    out_f = q.out_f
    y = torch.empty((4, out_f), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _kda_qkvg_kernel[(_ceil_div(out_f, 32),)](
        x, q.w_q, q.scales, q.zeros, k.w_q, k.scales, k.zeros,
        v.w_q, v.scales, v.zeros, g.w_q, g.scales, g.zeros, y,
        q.in_f, out_f, q.in_f // GROUP_SIZE, BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return y


def _experts_dual_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor, a, b) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
    n = idx.numel()
    ya = torch.empty((n, a.out_f), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    yb = torch.empty((n, b.out_f), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    _experts_dual_gemv_kernel[(n, _ceil_div(a.out_f, 32))](
        x, idx, a.w_q, a.scales, a.zeros, b.w_q, b.scales, b.zeros, ya, yb,
        a.in_f, a.out_f, a.in_f // GROUP_SIZE, BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return ya, yb


def _experts_down(h: torch.Tensor, coeff: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor, down, out: torch.Tensor,
                  add: bool) -> torch.Tensor:
    _experts_down_weighted_kernel[(_ceil_div(down.out_f, 32),)](
        h, coeff, idx, down.w_q, down.scales, down.zeros, out,
        down.in_f, down.out_f, down.in_f // GROUP_SIZE, idx.numel(), add,
        BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out


def _moe_dual_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor, gate, up, s_gate, s_up) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
    active = idx.numel()
    shared = s_gate.n
    rows = active + shared
    yg = torch.empty((rows, gate.out_f), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    yu = torch.empty((rows, up.out_f), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    _moe_dual_gemv_kernel[(rows, _ceil_div(gate.out_f, 32))](
        x, idx,
        gate.w_q, gate.scales, gate.zeros, up.w_q, up.scales, up.zeros,
        s_gate.w_q, s_gate.scales, s_gate.zeros, s_up.w_q, s_up.scales, s_up.zeros,
        yg, yu,
        gate.in_f, gate.out_f, gate.in_f // GROUP_SIZE, active, shared,
        BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return yg, yu


def _moe_down(h: torch.Tensor, coeff: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor, down, s_down) -> torch.Tensor:
    out = torch.empty((down.out_f,), device=h.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    active = idx.numel()
    shared = s_down.n
    _moe_down_kernel[(_ceil_div(down.out_f, 32),)](
        h, coeff, idx,
        down.w_q, down.scales, down.zeros, s_down.w_q, s_down.scales, s_down.zeros, out,
        down.in_f, down.out_f, down.in_f // GROUP_SIZE, active, shared,
        BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out


def _mla_q_abs(q_nope: torch.Tensor, kv_b) -> torch.Tensor:
    out = torch.empty((32, 512), device=q_nope.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _mla_q_abs_kernel[(32, _ceil_div(512, 32))](
        q_nope, kv_b.w_q, kv_b.scales, kv_b.zeros, out,
        32, 512, kv_b.out_f, BLOCK_K=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out


def _mla_v_out(ctx: torch.Tensor, kv_b) -> torch.Tensor:
    out = torch.empty((32, 128), device=ctx.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _mla_v_out_kernel[(32, _ceil_div(128, 32))](
        ctx, kv_b.w_q, kv_b.scales, kv_b.zeros, out,
        32, 512, kv_b.out_f, BLOCK_N=32, num_warps=4,
    )
    return out


def _pack_int4(w_q: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    lo = w_q[0::2] & 0xF
    hi = w_q[1::2] & 0xF
    return (lo | (hi << 4)).contiguous()


def quantize(w_io: torch.Tensor, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
    K, N = w_io.shape
    ng = K // group
    wg = w_io.view(ng, group, N).float()
    wmin = wg.min(dim=1, keepdim=True).values
    wmax = wg.max(dim=1, keepdim=True).values
    scales = (wmax - wmin).clamp_min(1e-8) / 15.0
    zeros = (-wmin / scales).round().clamp(0, 15)
    w_q = ((wg / scales) + zeros).round().clamp(0, 15).to(torch.uint8).view(K, N)
    return _pack_int4(w_q), scales.squeeze(1).to(torch.bfloat16), zeros.squeeze(1).to(torch.bfloat16)


class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        assert in_f % group == 0 and in_f % 2 == 0
        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

    def init_random(self, gen: torch.Generator, std: float = 0.02) -> None:
        w = torch.randn(self.in_f, self.out_f, generator=gen) * std
        wq, s, z = quantize(w, self.group)
        self.w_q.copy_(wq)
        self.scales.copy_(s)
        self.zeros.copy_(z)

    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        return _fused_gemv(x.contiguous(), self.w_q, self.scales, self.zeros, self.in_f, self.out_f)


class QuantExperts(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, n: int, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        self.n, self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = n, in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(n, in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

    def init_random(self, gen: torch.Generator, std: float = 0.02) -> None:
        for e in range(self.n):
            w = torch.randn(self.in_f, self.out_f, generator=gen) * std
            wq, s, z = quantize(w, self.group)
            self.w_q[e].copy_(wq)
            self.scales[e].copy_(s)
            self.zeros[e].copy_(z)


def _rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    if x.is_cuda:
        return _fused_rmsnorm(x, w)
    xf = x.float()
    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)


def _rope_cossin(pos: int, dim: int, theta: float, device):
    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
    ang = pos * inv
    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)


def _apply_rope(x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xf = x.float()
    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
    return out.to(x.dtype)


class KDA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, Dk, d = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.k_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.v_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.g_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.beta_proj = nn.Linear(d, H, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.conv_w = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(3, H * Dk, cfg.short_conv, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * Dk, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = Dk ** -0.5

    def _short_conv(self, val, prev, idx):
        return _fused_short_conv(val, prev, self.conv_w[idx])

    def step(self, x, st):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        qkvg = _kda_qkvg(x, self.q_proj, self.k_proj, self.v_proj, self.g_proj)
        q, k, v, g_raw = qkvg[0], qkvg[1], qkvg[2], qkvg[3]
        q, st["cq"] = self._short_conv(q, st["cq"], 0)
        k, st["ck"] = self._short_conv(k, st["ck"], 1)
        v, st["cv"] = self._short_conv(v, st["cv"], 2)
        q = q.view(H, Dk).float() * self.scale
        k = k.view(H, Dk).float()
        v = v.view(H, Dk).float()
        g = (-F.softplus(g_raw.float())).view(H, Dk)
        beta = torch.sigmoid(self.beta_proj(x).float())
        S = st["S"] * g.exp()[:, :, None]
        pred = (S * k[:, :, None]).sum(1)
        S = S + beta[:, None, None] * k[:, :, None] * (v - pred)[:, None, :]
        o = (S * q[:, :, None]).sum(1)
        st["S"] = S
        return self.o_proj(o.reshape(H * Dk).to(torch.bfloat16))


class MLA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, d = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope), cfg.group)
        self.kv_a = QuantLinear(d, cfg.kv_lora + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.group)
        self.kv_b = QuantLinear(cfg.kv_lora, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.group)
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * cfg.v_head, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope) ** -0.5

    def step(self, x, st):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H = cfg.mla_heads
        pos = st["c_kv"].shape[0]
        q = self.q_proj(x).view(H, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope)
        q_nope = q[:, : cfg.qk_nope]
        q_rope = q[:, cfg.qk_nope :]
        kv = self.kv_a(x)
        c_kv = kv[: cfg.kv_lora]
        k_rope = kv[cfg.kv_lora :]
        cos, sin = _rope_cossin(pos, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.rope_theta, x.device)
        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin)
        k_rope = _apply_rope(k_rope, cos, sin)
        st["c_kv"] = torch.cat([st["c_kv"], c_kv[None]], 0)
        st["k_rope"] = torch.cat([st["k_rope"], k_rope[None]], 0)

        q_abs = _mla_q_abs(q_nope, self.kv_b)
        scores = (q_abs @ st["c_kv"].t()).float()
        scores = scores + (q_rope.float() @ st["k_rope"].float().t())
        scores = scores * self.scale
        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=-1).to(torch.bfloat16)
        ctx = p @ st["c_kv"]
        o = _mla_v_out(ctx.contiguous(), self.kv_b)
        return self.o_proj(o.reshape(H * cfg.v_head))


class MoE(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        d, m, E = cfg.hidden, cfg.moe_inter, cfg.n_experts
        self.router = nn.Linear(d, E, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.gate = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.up = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.down = QuantExperts(E, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.s_gate = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_up = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_down = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.register_buffer("_shared_idx", torch.arange(cfg.n_shared, dtype=torch.int64), persistent=False)
        self.register_buffer("_shared_coeff", torch.ones(cfg.n_shared, dtype=torch.float32), persistent=False)

    def step(self, x):
        cfg = self.cfg
        probs = torch.softmax(self.router(x).float(), dim=-1)
        w, idx = torch.topk(probs, cfg.n_active)
        w = w / (w.sum() + 1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
        g, u = _moe_dual_gemv(x, idx, self.gate, self.up, self.s_gate, self.s_up)
        h = F.silu(g) * u
        out = _moe_down(h.contiguous(), w.contiguous(), idx, self.down, self.s_down)
        return out.to(torch.bfloat16)


class Block(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg, kind):
        super().__init__()
        self.kind = kind
        self.attn_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.moe_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.attn = KDA(cfg) if kind == "K" else MLA(cfg)
        self.moe = MoE(cfg)

    def step(self, x, st):
        h = x + self.attn.step(_rmsnorm(x, self.attn_norm), st)
        return h + self.moe.step(_rmsnorm(h, self.moe_norm))


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)

    def step(self, hidden, state):
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
        return hidden, state


def init_state(cfg: Config, context_len: int, seed: int) -> list:
    dev = torch.device("cuda:0")
    g = torch.Generator(device=dev).manual_seed(seed)
    H, Dk = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim
    C = H * Dk
    state = []
    for kind in cfg.pattern:
        if kind == "K":
            state.append({
                "S": torch.randn(H, Dk, Dk, device=dev, generator=g) * 0.05,
                "cq": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "ck": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "cv": torch.randn(cfg.short_conv - 1, C, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
            })
        else:
            state.append({
                "c_kv": torch.randn(context_len, cfg.kv_lora, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
                "k_rope": torch.randn(context_len, cfg.qk_rope, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.1,
            })
    return state


def init_token(cfg: Config, seed: int) -> torch.Tensor:
    dev = torch.device("cuda:0")
    g = torch.Generator(device=dev).manual_seed(seed + 1)
    return torch.randn(cfg.hidden, device=dev, generator=g, dtype=cfg.dtype) * 0.25

Rationale: opencode is a strong harness but its `@ai-sdk/openai-compatible` transport stalls intermittently (~1/3-1/2 of sessions); routing these models through Claude Code to the provider Anthropic endpoint bypasses that adapter. - Always container mode (`KBH_AGENT_CONTAINER=1`): isolated per-run workspace, native GPU, sessions overlap while GPU commands serialize through the lock. ## Hard-won gotchas - **Commit email MUST be `elliot@arledge.net`** or Vercel silently fails the build verification. The template-mutation guard auto-flags grader tampering. - `kb lint <run_id|--all>` is a static reward-hack TRIPWIRE: scans solution.py for the patterns we have caught by hand (input-identity memoization, stack/check.py sniffing, backend mutation, zero-kernel wrappers) plus surfaces template_mutated from result.json. They are what makes a post read as signal, not slop. - **Charts MUST use the website NVIDIA palette.** Import the shared theme, never hardcode colors: `from kbh_theme import C, SERIES, apply` (module at `x-article-images/kbh_theme.py`, mirrored on Mac at `~/dev/sites/kernelbench.com/x-article-images/`). Content is identical; format is plain markdown for any CLI. See [`CLAUDE.md`](./CLAUDE.md) for the canonical version. All rules there apply. Summary of the non-negotiables: - **uv only.** `uv run ...`, `uv add ...`, `uv pip install ...`. Never `pip` or bare `python`. - **Before committing:** `uv run ruff check . --fix && uv run pytest`. - **Do not edit `problems/*/solution.py`** — those are agent output. - **Do not modify `reference.py`, `check.py`, `benchmark.py`, `problem.yaml`, `shapes.py`, or `PROMPT.txt`** of an already-published problem unless intentionally versioning the benchmark/validation surface; `scripts/run_hard.sh` invalidates and restores runs where agents under test change them. - **Apply the torch 2.11 inductor CSE hotfix** via `./scripts/patch_torch.sh` after any `uv sync`. - **Z.ai GLM-5.1 Claude Code reruns:** use `zai-claude`; `scripts/run_hard.sh` sets `CLAUDE_CODE_DISABLE_EXPERIMENTAL_BETAS=1`, `CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_RETRIES=1000000`, `CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=128000`, and routes all Claude Code aliases, including Haiku / Explore / subagents, to `glm-5.1`. - **GPU work must go through `scripts/run_hard.sh`.** It creates archive-local workspaces, isolated CUDA/Triton/Torch caches, and a shared GPU lock so concurrent agent sweeps can edit in parallel while compile/check/benchmark work queues cleanly. - **Correctness includes numeric stress.** `check.py` reruns canonical shapes/seeds under problem-specific small/large activation or weight scales via `src/eval/numeric_stress.py`; `benchmark.py` still measures only the canonical performance deck. ## Quick actions ```bash uv sync ./scripts/patch_torch.sh ./scripts/run_hard.sh claude claude-opus-4-7 problems/01_qwen3_decode_block ``` ## Repo layout and adding a new problem See `CLAUDE.md` — everything there is authoritative. ## Current sweep context Use `scripts/run_hard.sh` for all model evals. It stages each problem under `outputs/runs/<run_id>/repo/problems/<problem_name>/`, copies immutable problem files, symlinks `src/`, copies project metadata, and sets per-run `TORCH_EXTENSIONS_DIR`, `TRITON_CACHE_DIR`, `CUDA_CACHE_PATH`, and temp dirs. It also wraps `uv`, `python`, `python3`, `nvidia-smi`, `ncu`, `nsys`, and `nvcc` behind `outputs/gpu.lock`. The wrapper is reentrant through `KBH_GPU_LOCK_HELD=1`; preserve that guard or `uv run python benchmark.py` can deadlock when child `nvcc` tries to acquire the same lock. Run metadata includes agent wall time, total/check/benchmark wall time, check/benchmark exit codes, parsed token/cache/reasoning usage, and GPU lock wait/active totals via `scripts/summarize_runs.py`. Each `result.json` also includes `failure_reason` and `retryable_infra_failure`; the website should show these instead of flattening every non-pass into the same red cell. No-solution rows with fewer than 5,000 output tokens are treated as `provider_early_stop` and retryable by default. Provider-credit detection must stay credit-specific; do not match plain `overage`, because ordinary model text like `coverage` will false-positive. Provider credit/rate classifications should only apply to rows without a solution; successful sessions may quote old run logs or result JSON in the transcript, and those quotes are not provider failures. Provider credit/rate detection must read explicit CLI/API error events and stderr only, not arbitrary assistant text or tool outputs; models can read AGENTS.md, `run_hard.sh`, and old artifacts containing those trigger words. When `KBH_DISABLE_AGENT_CUDA=1`, agent-phase `uv`/`python`/`python3`, `nvidia-smi`, and `nvcc` probes bypass the lock because CUDA is hidden and guarded or the probe is harmless; `ncu` and `nsys` fail fast. Harness-owned `check.py`/`benchmark.py` still lock normally. The `check.py`/`benchmark.py` execution timeout must start after the GPU lock is acquired. Use `run_gpu_locked_timeout`; do not wrap `timeout` outside `uv run` or queued rows can fail while merely waiting for `outputs/gpu.lock`. `benchmark.py` must score `variant=solution` first. Eager / compiled / SOTA reference diagnostics are opt-in via `KBH_BENCHMARK_BASELINES=1` (or a per-problem alias) and emit `benchmark_event` start/end/error lines for audits. Transcript usage extraction also bypasses the lock; it is CPU-only post-processing. `check.py` numeric stress is part of official correctness and should stay on. `KBH_NUMERIC_STRESS=0` is for local debugging only, not sweeps or published backfills. These stress cases do not add hidden shapes; they rescale existing floating inputs/state to catch zero-output, cached-nominal, and loose-tolerance cheats. Before expensive sweeps, check: ```bash overnight-compute status nvidia-smi ``` The lock only protects KernelBench children launched through this harness. It does not stop unrelated CUDA compiles or benchmark jobs elsewhere on Anvil. For parallel sweeps, prefer: ```bash KBH_DISABLE_AGENT_CUDA=1 ./scripts/launch_parallel_sweep.sh ``` `scripts/launch_parallel_sweep.sh` defaults to `KBH_HARNESS_CONCURRENCY=2`, so each harness/provider path gets at most two active agent sessions at once. Raise it only after a preflight proves quota and rate limits are healthy. The launcher must use per-harness workers. A problem-major loop causes head-of-line blocking: if Codex or Claude holds its two slots, freed Cursor, Gemini, or OpenCode slots do not backfill. Run `./scripts/preflight_harnesses.sh` before expensive sweeps; it sends tiny text prompts through the current matrix and fails fast on auth/quota/model-route problems. After a sweep, `./scripts/launch_infra_retries.sh <run_group>` reruns only rows where `result.json` has `retryable_infra_failure=true`, such as provider rate limits, early stops, or no-solution timeouts. user
I need you to make batch-1 autoregressive decode of a Kimi-Linear hybrid block as fast as possible on the RTX PRO 6000 (SM120 Blackwell, GDDR7, 1.8 TB/s). The model is W4A16: the big projection weights are stored as 4-bit integers, the activations and accumulation are bf16. reference.py is the correctness oracle and baseline.py is an already-optimized pure-PyTorch version; your job is to go beyond baseline.py. Your answer goes in solution.py and must expose the same Model class and the same step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state) interface as reference.py, with identical buffer/parameter names so it loads the reference weights. Make whatever mess you want in this directory otherwise. The unit is one repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B: four layers in the pattern [KDA, KDA, KDA, MLA], each followed by a 64-expert MoE FFN (top-8 routed + 1 shared, SiLU, intermediate 1024), with RMSNorm and residuals. Hidden size is 2304. The KDA layers are gated-delta linear attention with 32 heads of dim 128, a short causal depthwise conv (kernel 4) on q/k/v, a per-channel log-decay gate, and a per-head write strength; they carry a fixed-size recurrent state S[32,128,128] plus the conv window across decode steps. The MLA layers are multi-head latent attention with 32 heads, a kv_lora_rank of 512, qk_nope 128, qk_rope 64, v_head 128, decoupled RoPE (theta 10000); they carry a growing compressed latent KV cache (the 512-d latent plus the 64-d rope key per past token). The weights are quantized W4A16, AWQ/GPTQ-style: per linear, the (in, out) weight is stored as int4 packed two-per-byte along `in` (w_q, uint8, shape (in//2, out)), with per-group asymmetric dequant params group-size 128 along `in` (scales and zeros, bf16, shape (in//128, out)). Dequant is w[k,n] = (unpack(w_q)[k,n] - zeros[k//128,n]) * scales[k//128,n]. The 64 MoE experts (and the shared expert) are stored the same way, one int4 weight set per expert. reference.py has the exact pack/unpack/dequant code, the layer math, the state layout, and how step consumes one token and updates both kinds of state. Read it. At batch 1 this decode is bandwidth-bound on the weight stream, and the int4 weights are a quarter of the bytes of bf16 - but only if you never materialize the dequantized bf16 weight. reference.py and baseline.py both unpack each weight to a full bf16 matrix and then matmul, which throws the bandwidth advantage away (int4 read plus bf16 write plus bf16 read). The job is to fuse the int4 unpack and per-group dequant directly into the GEMV so you stream the int4 weights once. You are decoding one new token against a context that is already `context_len` tokens long (the states and caches are pre-filled). Correctness is the next-token hidden vector and the updated decode state matching reference.py by cosine similarity (>= 0.98), checked from an identical fed state across several seeds and context lengths. You are scored on decode latency relative to baseline.py, geomean over context lengths 2048, 8192, and 16384. This needs to be real. Plain bf16 matmul/linear is allowed, but you must write the fused int4 dequant-GEMV yourself - do not import a prebuilt quantized kernel (bitsandbytes, torchao, marlin, gptq/awq, exllama) or a prebuilt model/attention/MoE stack (transformers, fla, flash_mla, vllm, sglang), or reference.py / baseline.py. If you need background, look up W4A16 / AWQ / GPTQ dequant-GEMV kernels, the Kimi-Linear architecture, KDA / gated DeltaNet, multi-head latent attention, and Blackwell/Triton decode kernels yourself. Your flywheel is implement, profile (ncu, nsys, torch.profiler - whatever helps) and time it with benchmark.py, verify correctness by running `python check.py` and reading the output, then iterate. Do not substitute your own one-off checks for check.py - it tests every layer type and the state update across seeds, your spot-check almost certainly will not. If `python check.py` has not printed PASS, you are not done. Take as long as you need to actually push the latency down. Correctness oracle, NOT the fast baseline (baseline.py) or the SOTA ceiling.

format that open-source inference actually ships).

Why W4A16 and not fp8: at batch-1 decode the bottleneck is *weight memory
traffic*. int4 weights are 0.25x the bytes of bf16 (4x less traffic), and a
fused dequant-GEMV realizes that win in the memory-bound regime where decode
lives -- unlike fp8 tensor-core matmul, which has fixed overhead and loses at
M=1. int4/bf16-acc also needs no special tensor-core format, so it runs on any
bf16-capable GPU (Ampere, Hopper, Blackwell).

The two decode states are unchanged: KDA carries a fixed-size recurrent state
S[H,Dk,Dv] + short-conv window; MLA carries a growing compressed latent KV
cache. `step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state)` consumes one token.

This reference dequantizes naively (unpack -> bf16 matrix -> matmul). The whole
problem is to FUSE the int4 unpack+dequant into the GEMV and never materialize
the bf16 weight. Pack format is identical to KernelBench-Hard proble

The floor the solution must beat -- NOT the oracle (reference.py). Same int4

def _wbf(ql) -> torch.Tensor:
    return ql.weight_bf()  # [in, out] bf16

"""Correctness runner for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.

Per-step correctness, not a chained trajectory: for each seed and a couple of
context lengths, the reference and the solution are given an IDENTICAL fed
state and one new token, each runs ONE decode step, and we compare the

"""Latency benchmark for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.

Score = baseline_latency / solution_latency (speedup over the optimized-PyTorch
baseline.py), geomean over the context-length sweep. The solution is timed
first; a final next-token check against the reference makes a fast-but-wrong
solution score zero. Absolute tok/s at the longest context is the shippable
"single-GPU decode" number.

Reported in the peak_fraction field as a speedup multiple (>1 means faster than
the baseline), not a [0,1] roofline fraction.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import sys
import time
from math import exp, log
from pathlib import Path

import torch
import yaml


def _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
    h = ref.init_token(cfg, seed)
    st = ref.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
    with torch.no_grad():
        for _ in range(steps):
            h, st = model.step(h, st)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    return h


def _time(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
    _run(model, cfg, ctx, min(3, steps), seed, ref)   # warmup
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    best = float("inf")
    for _ in range(int(yaml.safe_load(Path("problem.yaml").read_text()).get("num_perf_trials", 3))):
        t0 = time.perf_counter()
        h = _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref)
        best = min(best, time.perf_counter() - t0)
    return best, h

"""Decode shapes for the Kimi-Linear hybrid unit.

Score is latency speedup over baseline.py, so the sweep is over decode context
length. The long-context shape is where the architecture's design (fixed-size
KDA state + compressed MLA latent cache) pays off and where the absorb-vs-
materialize fork in MLA decides the whole thing -- that is the shippable "wow".

+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+OP_TYPE = "kimi_linear_w4a16_decode"
+HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000"]
+EPS = 1.0e-6
+GROUP_SIZE = 128
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class Config:
+    hidden: int = 2304
+    kda_heads: int = 32
+    kda_head_dim: int = 128
+    short_conv: int = 4
+    mla_heads: int = 32
+    kv_lora: int = 512
+    qk_nope: int = 128
+    qk_rope: int = 64
+    v_head: int = 128
+    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
+    n_experts: int = 64
+    n_active: int = 8
+    n_shared: int = 1
+    moe_inter: int = 1024
+    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
+    group: int = 128
+    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
+    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)
+
+
+def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
+    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _int4_gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                      BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+
+    for g in range(0, NG):
+        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
+        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+        packed = tl.load(wq + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
+                         mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+        s = tl.load(scales + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(zeros + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += s * (qx - z * xs)
+
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _experts_dual_gemv_kernel(x, idx, wq_a, scales_a, zeros_a, wq_b, scales_b, zeros_b, y_a, y_b,
+                              K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                              BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc_a = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc_b = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
+    q_base = e * NG * N
+
+    for g in range(0, NG):
+        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
+        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+        w_offs = w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
+
+        pa = tl.load(wq_a + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        loa = (pa & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hia = ((pa >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qxa = tl.sum(loa * xe[:, None] + hia * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        sa = tl.load(scales_a + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        za = tl.load(zeros_a + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc_a += sa * (qxa - za * xs)
+
+        pb = tl.load(wq_b + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lob = (pb & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hib = ((pb >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qxb = tl.sum(lob * xe[:, None] + hib * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        sb = tl.load(scales_b + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zb = tl.load(zeros_b + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc_b += sb * (qxb - zb * xs)
+
+    tl.store(y_a + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_a, mask=mask_n)
+    tl.store(y_b + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_b, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _experts_down_weighted_kernel(h, coeff, idx, wq, scales, zeros, y,
+                                  K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                                  ESEL: tl.constexpr, ADD: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+
+    for ep in range(0, ESEL):
+        e = tl.load(idx + ep)
+        c = tl.load(coeff + ep).to(tl.float32)
+        w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
+        q_base = e * NG * N
+        acc_e = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+        for g in range(0, NG):
+            k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+            xe = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
+            xo = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+            packed = tl.load(wq + w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
+                             mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+            lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
+            hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+            qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+            xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+            s = tl.load(scales + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            z = tl.load(zeros + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            acc_e += s * (qx - z * xs)
+        acc += c * acc_e
+
+    if ADD:
+        acc += tl.load(y + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _mla_q_abs_kernel(q, wq, scales, zeros, out,
+                      H: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_h = tl.program_id

reasoning (461 chars)
**Analyzing CUDA kernel performance** **Evaluating kernel call consolidation** **Optimizing MoE kernel launches** **Analyzing kernel fusion trade-offs** I'm weighing the benefits of reducing kernel launches by fusing MoE operations against the added code complexity and potential performance costs, while also considering softmax optimization possibilities to improve attention efficiency. **Optimizing softmax computation** **Verifying memory layout changes**
assistant
The profiler shows the long-context MLA softmax is expensive because the score tensor is laid out as `[length, heads]` and softmax runs down the strided dimension. I’m flipping MLA scores to `[heads, length]` so softmax runs over a contiguous last dimension, while keeping the same latent formulation.

model.load_state_dict(ref_model.state_dict(), strict=True)

st = reference.init_state(cfg, 8192, 11)
with torch.no_grad():
    for _ in range(5):
        h, st = model.step(h, st)

        torch.cuda.synchronize()

+@triton.jit
+def _experts_down_weighted_kernel(h, coeff, idx, wq, scales, zeros, y,
+                                  K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                                  ESEL: tl.constexpr, ADD: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _moe_dual_gemv_kernel(x, idx,
+                          wq_a, scales_a, zeros_a, wq_b, scales_b, zeros_b,
+                          swq_a, sscales_a, szeros_a, swq_b, sscales_b, szeros_b,
+                          y_a, y_b,
+                          K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                          ACTIVE: tl.constexpr, SHARED: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    is_routed = pid_e < ACTIVE
+    e_r = tl.load(idx + pid_e, mask=is_routed, other=0)
+    e_s = pid_e - ACTIVE
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc_a = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc_b = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    w_base_r = e_r * (K // 2) * N
+    q_base_r = e_r * NG * N
+    w_base_s = e_s * (K // 2) * N
+    q_base_s = e_s * NG * N
+
+    for g in range(0, NG):
+        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
+        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+        w_offs_r = w_base_r + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
+        w_offs_s = w_base_s + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
+        ptra = tl.where(is_routed, wq_a + w_offs_r, swq_a + w_offs_s)
+        ptrb = tl.where(is_routed, wq_b + w_offs_r, swq_b + w_offs_s)
+
+        pa = tl.load(ptra, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        loa = (pa & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hia = ((pa >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qxa = tl.sum(loa * xe[:, None] + hia * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ptra_s = tl.where(is_routed, scales_a + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
+                          sscales_a + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
+        ptra_z = tl.where(is_routed, zeros_a + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
+                          szeros_a + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
+        sa = tl.load(ptra_s, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        za = tl.load(ptra_z, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc_a += sa * (qxa - za * xs)
+
+        pb = tl.load(ptrb, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lob = (pb & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hib = ((pb >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qxb = tl.sum(lob * xe[:, None] + hib * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ptrb_s = tl.where(is_routed, scales_b + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
+                          sscales_b + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
+        ptrb_z = tl.where(is_routed, zeros_b + q_base_r + g * N + offs_n,
+                          szeros_b + q_base_s + g * N + offs_n)
+        sb = tl.load(ptrb_s, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zb = tl.load(ptrb_z, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc_b += sb * (qxb - zb * xs)
+
+    tl.store(y_a + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_a, mask=mask_n)
+    tl.store(y_b + pid_e * N + offs_n, acc_b, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _moe_down_kernel(h, coeff, idx,
+                     wq, scales, zeros, swq, sscales, szeros, y,
+                     K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                     ACTIVE: tl.constexpr, SHARED: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+
+    for ep in range(0, ACTIVE + SHARED):
+        if ep < ACTIVE:
+            e = tl.load(idx + ep)
+            c = tl.load(coeff + ep).to(tl.float32)
+            base_w = wq
+            base_s = scales
+            base_z = zeros
+        else:
+            e = ep - ACTIVE
+            c = 1.0
+            base_w = swq
+            base_s = sscales
+            base_z = szeros
+        w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
+        q_base = e * NG * N
+        acc_e = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+        for g in range(0, NG):
+            k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+            xe = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
+            xo = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+            packed = tl.load(base_w + w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
+                             mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+            lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
+            hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+            qx = tl.sum(lo * xe[:, None] + hi * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+            xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+            s = tl.load(base_s + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            z = tl.load(base_z + q_base + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+            acc_e += s * (qx - z * xs)
+        acc += c * acc_e
+
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _mla_q_abs_kernel(q, wq, scales, zeros, out,
+                      H: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+def _experts_down(h: torch.Tensor, coeff: torch.Tensor, idx: torch.Tensor, down, out: torch.Tensor,
+                  add: boo

@triton.jit
def _moe_down_kernel(h, coeff, idx,
                     wq, scales, zeros, swq, sscales, szeros, y,
                     K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                     ACTIVE: tl.constexpr, SHARED: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    mask_n = offs_n < N
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)

    for ep in range(0, ACTIVE + SHARED):
        if ep < ACTIVE:
            e = tl.load(idx + ep)
            c = tl.load(coeff + ep).to(tl.float32)
            base_w = wq
            base_s = scales
            base_z = zeros
        else:
            e = tl.full((), ep - ACTIVE, tl.int64)
            c = 1.0
            base_w = swq
            base_s = sscales
            base_z = szeros
        w_base = e * (K // 2) * N
        q_base = e * NG * N
        acc_e = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
        for g in range(0, NG):
            k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
            xe = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0).to(tl.float32)
            xo = tl.load(h + ep * K + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
            packed = tl.load(base_w + w_base + (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                             mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
            lo = (packed & 15).to(tl.float32)
            hi = ((packed >> 4) & 15).to(t

+def _kda_qkvg_kernel(x,
+                     wq0, s0, z0, wq1, s1, z1, wq2, s2, z2, wq3, s3, z3, y,
+                     K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    mask_n = offs_n < N
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc2 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc3 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+
+    for g in range(0, NG):
+        k0 = g * 128 + offs_p * 2
+        xe = tl.load(x + k0).to(tl.float32)
+        xo = tl.load(x + k0 + 1).to(tl.float32)
+        xs = tl.sum(xe + xo, axis=0)
+        w_offs = (g * 64 + offs_p)[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :]
+
+        p0 = tl.load(wq0 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lo0 = (p0 & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi0 = ((p0 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qx0 = tl.sum(lo0 * xe[:, None] + hi0 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ss0 = tl.load(s0 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zz0 = tl.load(z0 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc0 += ss0 * (qx0 - zz0 * xs)
+
+        p1 = tl.load(wq1 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lo1 = (p1 & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi1 = ((p1 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qx1 = tl.sum(lo1 * xe[:, None] + hi1 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ss1 = tl.load(s1 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zz1 = tl.load(z1 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc1 += ss1 * (qx1 - zz1 * xs)
+
+        p2 = tl.load(wq2 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lo2 = (p2 & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi2 = ((p2 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qx2 = tl.sum(lo2 * xe[:, None] + hi2 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ss2 = tl.load(s2 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zz2 = tl.load(z2 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc2 += ss2 * (qx2 - zz2 * xs)
+
+        p3 = tl.load(wq3 + w_offs, mask=mask_n[None, :], other=0)
+        lo3 = (p3 & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi3 = ((p3 >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        qx3 = tl.sum(lo3 * xe[:, None] + hi3 * xo[:, None], axis=0)
+        ss3 = tl.load(s3 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        zz3 = tl.load(z3 + g * N + offs_n, mask=mask_n, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc3 += ss3 * (qx3 - zz3 * xs)
+
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc0, mask=mask_n)
+    tl.store(y + N + offs_n, acc1, mask=mask_n)
+    tl.store(y + 2 * N + offs_n, acc2, mask=mask_n)
+    tl.store(y + 3 * N + offs_n, acc3, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _experts_dual_gemv_kernel(x, idx, wq_a, scales_a, zeros_a, wq_b, scales_b, zeros_b, y_a, y_b,

+@triton.jit
+def _int4_gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                      BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=mask_n)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _rmsnorm_kernel(x, w, y, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    mask = offs < N
+    xv = tl.load(x + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    wv = tl.load(w + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    ss = tl.sum(xv * xv, axis=0) / N
+    inv = tl.rsqrt(ss + 1.0e-6)
+    tl.store(y + offs, xv * inv * wv, mask=mask)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kda_qkvg_kernel(x,
+def _ceil_div(a: int, b: int) -> int:
+    return triton.cdiv(a, b)
+
+
+def _fused_rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    y = torch.empty_like(x)
+    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, y, x.numel(), BLOCK=4096, num_warps=8)
+    return y
+
+
+def _fused_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, wq: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor,
+                in_f: int, out_f: int) -> torch.Tensor:

+@triton.jit
+def _rmsnorm_kernel(x, w, y, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    tl.store(y + offs, xv * inv * wv, mask=mask)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _short_conv_kernel(val, prev, weight, out, new_prev, C: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs = pid * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    mask = offs < C
+    p0 = tl.load(prev + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p1 = tl.load(prev + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p2 = tl.load(prev + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    x = tl.load(val + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w0 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w1 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w2 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w3 = tl.load(weight + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    y = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + x * w3
+    y = y * tl.sigmoid(y)
+    tl.store(out + offs, y, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(new_prev + offs, p1, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(new_prev + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(new_prev + 2 * C + offs, x, mask=mask)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kda_qkvg_kernel(x,
+def _fused_rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    return y
+
+
+def _fused_short_conv(val: torch.Tensor, prev: torch.Tensor, weight: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
+    out = torch.empty_like(val)
+    new_prev = torch.empty_like(prev)
+    _short_conv_kernel[(_ceil_div(val.numel(), 256),)](
+        val, prev, weight, out, new_prev, val.numel(), BLOCK=256, num_warps=4,
+    )
+    return out, new_prev
+

+                      H: tl.constexpr, D: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_DV: tl.constexpr):
+    h = tl.program_id(0)
+    block_v = tl.program_id(1)
+    offs_v = block_v * BLOCK_DV + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_DV)
+    mask_v = offs_v < D
+    base_h = h * D * D
+    base_vec = h * D
+    pred = tl.zeros((BLOCK_DV,), tl.float32)
+
+    for dk in range(0, D):
+        gg = tl.load(g + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
+        kk = tl.load(k + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
+        s_old = tl.load(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        pred += (s_old * tl.exp(gg)) * kk
+
+    vv = tl.load(v + base_vec + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    bb = tl.load(beta + h).to(tl.float32)
+    oacc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_DV,), tl.float32)
+
+    for dk in range(0, D):
+        gg = tl.load(g + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
+        kk = tl.load(k + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
+        qq = tl.load(q + base_vec + dk).to(tl.float32)
+        s_old = tl.load(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, mask=mask_v, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        s_new = s_old * tl.exp(gg) + bb * kk * (vv - pred)
+        tl.store(S + base_h + dk * D + offs_v, s_new, mask=mask_v)
+        oacc += s_new * qq
+
+    tl.store(out + base_vec + offs_v, oacc, mask=mask_v)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _kda_qkvg_kernel(x,
+def _fused_short_conv(val: torch.Tensor, prev: torch.Tensor, weight: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
+    return out, new_prev
+
+
+def _fused_kda_state(q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, g: torch.Tensor,
+                     beta: torch.Tensor, state_s: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    out = torch.empty((32, 128), device=q.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    _kda_state_kernel[(32, 4)](
+        q, k, v, g, beta, state_s, out,
+        32, 128, BLOCK_DV=32, num_warps=4,
+    )
+    return out
+
+
+def _fused_gemv(x: torch.Tensor, wq: torch.Tensor, scales: torch.Tensor, zeros: torch.Tensor,
